```diff
+            volume_pyhalo += geo.volume_element_comoving(z[i], delta_z)
+
+        ds = self.cosmo.D_C_z(1.5)
+        volume_true = 1./3 * np.pi * radius_radians ** 2 * ds ** 3
+        npt.assert_almost_equal(volume_true, volume_pyhalo, 3)
+
 
 if __name__ == '__main__':
       pytest.main()
```
